SECTION 1: Ordering Instructions

Agencies should follow the steps below to streamline the ordering of PCs and related peripherals and value-added services under the PC Volume Purchase Master Award.

Please note: Requisitions no longer need to be sent to the Statewide IT Procurement Office prior to ordering if your orders are placed via E-Procurement. If you do not use E-Procurement, please email a copy of your request to beverly.satterfield@nc.gov for tracking purposes.

  • Purchase Orders for purchases under this Volume Purchasing Award must be sent to the ordering addresses in the table below.
Table: Vendor, Ordering Address, Ordering Contact and Order Status Inquiries

2. When ordering, IT IS CRITICAL THAT YOU INCLUDE ALL OF THE REQUIRED INFORMATION NOTED BELOW ON YOUR PURCHASE ORDER:

Table: Field, Instructions
FieldInstructions
PO CommentsReference “NCBB Order and Master Quote 501326”. (Note: Select 204A as Contract number on E-Procurement requisitions.)
Vendor CommentsPlease provide the email address and phone number of the vendor to whom the Customer should contact with any questions regarding your purchase order.
Line Item Description for Desktops, Portables, and MonitorsInclude Configuration Name exactly as it appears in Section 2 (e.g., Item 1.1a Standard Desktop (256GB SSD, Intel Proc)) AND Vendor Part Number from Section 2. NOTE: Agencies may order any of the Monitor configurations from any of the awarded vendors.
Line Item Description for 2-in-1 Laptop / TabletIf you are ordering a 2-in-1 Laptop/Tablet without wireless wide area network (WWAN) capability (e.g., you only require Wi-Fi and no data plan), then your line-item description should include “3.1a 2-in-1 Laptop / Tablet (Non-vPro) (No WWAN)” AND the Vendor Part Number from Section 2. If you need a 2-in-1 Laptop/Tablets with WWAN capability from either AT&T, Verizon, or T-Mobile, include the appropriate configuration name AND Vendor Part Number from Section 2. Note that Dell, HP, Lenovo, & Microsoft may have different Vendor Part Numbers for the four configuration options under the 2-in-1 Laptops / Tablets Segment. When ordering a WWAN model of the 2-in-1 Laptop/Tablet, note in the line-item description if Agency is requesting the AT&T, T-Mobile, or Verizon model. To obtain AT&T, T-Mobile, or Verizon data service for your 2-in-2 Laptop/Tablet, you should use the 915A IT Statewide Term Contract for Cellular Services.
Line Item Description for OptionsThe Awarded Pricing list in Section 2 includes Options that are available for Vendors’ awarded configurations. Be sure to include in the line-item description the Option Item Description (e.g., Nylon Carrying Case) and Vendor Part Number as they appear in this document. Please closely review the listed Option items to make sure you are ordering the correct Option for the Desktop, Portable, or 2-in-1 Laptop / Tablet configuration and Vendor that are listed on your requisition.
Special Instructions or Order Status InquiriesJust like any other normal procurement, if you have specific delivery instructions or delivery requirements (e.g., no loading dock, inside delivery required), you must include them in the Vendor Comments on your Purchase Orders. Also, please contact the appropriate awarded vendor and notify them of any special delivery requirements. If you have multiple ship-to locations on your purchase orders, please contact the awarded vendor to ensure that the order is correctly designated in the Vendor’s system.

3. **Warranty Information:** All configurations in the Desktop, Portable, and 2-in-1 Laptop/Tablet Segments come standard with a 3-Year, Next Business Day On-Site with Defective Hard Drive Retention Warranty. If you wish to purchase an extended or upgraded warranty, then you will need to select the applicable extended/upgraded warranty option from the list of Options for the applicable model and add it as an additional line item on your requisition. Be sure to include in the Line-Item Description the Option Item Description (e.g., 4th Year Next Business Day, On-site w/hard drive retention warranty) and Vendor Part Number as they appear in this document. Please note: Dell will add the cost of an extended warranty into the total cost of the device when it is invoiced. The extended warranty options will not be a separate line item on Dell’s invoices. Agencies should contact Dell to get a quote for the device with any extended or upgraded warranty included in the pricing.

All configurations in the Monitors Segment come standard with a 3-Year, Advanced Exchange NBD warranty. There are no upgrade or extended warranty options for monitors under this award.

4. **Operating System Information**: All Dell, HP, Lenovo, and Microsoft Device Configurations ship with Windows 11 Pro 64-Bit ONLY.

5. **Resource Media**: Agencies may download Resource Media from the Vendors’ websites.

  • For Dell – Go to
  • For HP – Agencies can download individual drivers at
  • For Lenovo – Go to
  • For Microsoft - Go to

6. **Value Added Services**: If you are ordering any of the Value-Added Services such as Custom Imaging, Asset Tagging, Installation, or Managed Logistics / Staggered Delivery, then you must contact the Vendor prior to issuing your purchase order. These Value-Added Services require the Agency to provide the Vendor with additional information in advance (e.g., Agency must provide Vendor with their Pre-Certified Custom Image and / or Asset Tags). There is additional order processing time involved with the initial set-up and testing of a Custom Image and Asset Tagging. See Table 1 below for Vendor Part Numbers and Not-To-Exceed unit pricing for Value Added Services available under this award. **Additional Value-Added Services may be offered by the Vendors upon request.**

Table: Value Added Service Option, Dell, HP, Lenovo, and 1 more column

*Table 1: Value Added Services Vendor Part Numbers and Not-To-Exceed Unit Prices*

7. **Order Delivery**: The standard delivery for orders issued under the Volume Purchase is within 21 days after Vendor’s receipt of purchase order. Please note: Occasional worldwide component shortages may cause shipping delays for devices and certain options (specifically laptops, monitors, and docking stations).

8. **Volume Purchase Master Award and Volume Purchase Procedures**: The most current versions of the Volume Purchase Master Award and Volume Purchase Procedures are located at the following website: http://it.nc.gov/statewide-programs/it-volume-purchasing (opens in new window). The Volume Purchase Master Award is updated frequently due to Vendor product updates, so please use the most current version of the Volume Purchase Master Award posted on this site when placing an order.

9. **Questions**: Please email Beverly Satterfield at beverly.satterfield@nc.gov if you have any additional questions or issues. If you have an issue or question about an existing order, please include your purchase order number and the order date in your email.
